18–19 Point Pioneer Decks from Players Tour Brussels 2020












18–19 Point Pioneer Decks
-------------------------


The players of the following decks got six match wins and a draw out of the ten Pioneer rounds.








#### Bastogne, Jerome - Azorius Control


#####
